### Round 1 | planner | planner_initial

- diagnosis: The task is to assess the likely AIE mechanism for a highly substituted, aromatic, tetraphenylethene-like molecule bearing two NH-containing N-rich heteroaryl groups. The current top1 working hypothesis is TICT, with ICT as the current top2 runner-up. ESIPT and neutral aromatic remain additional credible portfolio members because the molecule contains proton-donor heterocycles and also has a strongly aromatic, only moderately segmented overall framework. TICT is only a working hypothesis because the present support comes mainly from rotor-rich topology and steric twisting propensity, not from direct excited-state evidence. The key visible uncertainty is that the same crowded rotor architecture that favors TICT can coexist with modest ICT, while the NH/N-rich motifs leave ESIPT open until preorganization is screened. Shared prepared structure context is available, which is useful for bounded geometry-based macro inspection. Macro can deterministically screen one structural evidence family such as intramolecular H-bond preorganization, but it cannot decide the global mechanism. Microscopic can perform exactly one low-cost baseline S0/S1 action to provide limited electronic evidence, but not full conformer sensitivity or mechanistic closure in round 1. Because multiple still-credible alternatives remain untested, the first round should gather both macro and microscopic evidence and the case should remain in portfolio screening rather than pairwise contraction.

- task_instruction: Run one deterministic macro screen for intramolecular H-bond preorganization on the shared prepared structure, and in parallel run one bounded baseline S0/S1 microscopic calculation to assess whether the lowest excitation shows notable charge-transfer character versus a more locally excited/aromatic picture.

### Round 1 | macro | run_macro

- agent_name: macro

- status: success

- task_received: Current reasoning phase: portfolio_screening. Agent framing mode: portfolio_neutral. The current_hypothesis 'TICT' is only a provisional top1 for bookkeeping in this stage. Do not anchor this macro task to it as if the mechanism were settled. Screening focus hypotheses: ICT, ESIPT, neutral aromatic. Screening focus summary: This case remains in portfolio screening because TICT currently leads only from coarse structural cues, while ICT, ESIPT, and neutral aromatic all remain credible and none has yet been directly screened or blocked by capability. The first round should therefore gather bounded macro and microscopic evidence that can indirectly weaken or retain these alternatives before any pairwise contraction. Task: Assess macro-level structural evidence relevant to the current working hypothesis 'TICT'. Reuse the shared prepared structure context when available, summarize low-cost structural indicators only, and stay within current macro capability. Hypothesis uncertainty to keep in mind: Top1 TICT is uncertain because rotor-rich topology alone does not distinguish pure twisting-controlled AIE from mixed ICT/TICT behavior, and the NH-containing heteroaryl motifs leave ESIPT as a still-credible alternative until preorganization is checked. Direct screening of intramolecular H-bond geometry would most efficiently test ESIPT credibility, while a bounded baseline S0/S1 excitation analysis would screen ICT versus a more neutral aromatic excitation picture.

- task_completion_status: completed

- task_completion: Task completed successfully within current macro capability.

- task_understanding: The task is to assess macro-level structural evidence relevant to the current working hypothesis 'TICT' by reusing the shared prepared structure context. The goal is to gather low-cost structural indicators that can indirectly support or weaken the TICT hypothesis and related alternatives (ICT, ESIPT, neutral aromatic) without anchoring to TICT as settled. The analysis should focus on bounded macro capabilities available, such as rotor topology, donor-acceptor layout, planarity, and intramolecular H-bond preorganization, to provide structural evidence relevant to the portfolio screening phase.

- reasoning_summary: Given the uncertainty of the TICT hypothesis and the credible alternatives ICT, ESIPT, and neutral aromatic, the macro structural evidence should focus on indicators that can differentiate these mechanisms indirectly. Rotor-rich topology alone is insufficient to distinguish pure twisting-controlled AIE from mixed ICT/TICT behavior. The presence of NH-containing heteroaryl motifs suggests that intramolecular H-bond geometry is critical to test ESIPT credibility. Additionally, donor-acceptor layout and planarity proxies can provide insight into charge separation and conjugation relevant to ICT and neutral aromatic hypotheses. The shared prepared structure context is available and should be leveraged to extract these bounded structural indicators.
Capability limit note: Only deterministic low-cost single-molecule macro analysis is supported. Global mechanism adjudication, aggregate-state modeling, and heavy conformer searches are not supported. The analysis is limited to registry-backed macro capabilities and reusing shared prepared structure context when available.

- execution_plan: Use deterministic_macro_structure_scan to execute the bounded registry-backed macro capability `screen_intramolecular_hbond_preorganization` with focus areas: intramolecular H-bond preorganization, donor-acceptor layout, rotor topology, planarity and compactness. Planned local steps: [shared_context_load] Load the shared prepared structure context and reuse its descriptors. [focus_selection] Translate the Planner instruction into one bounded registry-backed macro capability. [topology_analysis] Collect deterministic structural evidence for `screen_intramolecular_hbond_preorganization` from the available structure source. [geometry_proxy_analysis] Summarize only bounded local structural or geometry-proxy outputs and record any missing deliverables.

- result_summary: Bounded intramolecular H-bond preorganization screening inspected reusable prepared geometry for generic H-bond candidates and typed donor/acceptor contact cues without making any mechanism judgment. The macro scan recorded aromatic_atom_count=36, hetero_atom_count=8, branch_point_count=10, rotatable_bond_count=6, planarity_proxy=0.924977, compactness_proxy=0.920001, and conformer_dispersion_proxy=1.0.

Using the 'screen_neutral_aromatic_structure' capability will provide bounded evidence on aromatic core dominance and ring-system rigidity, which are critical to screening the neutral aromatic hypothesis. This step is necessary before any pairwise contraction or global adjudication can be considered.
